function onBefore() { 
		image = this.id;
		changeClass(image);
                
//		if(image == 6){
//			document.getElementById('Link01').style.display = 'block';
//			document.getElementById('Link02').style.display = 'block';
//		}else{
//			document.getElementById('Link01').style.display = 'none';
//			document.getElementById('Link02').style.display = 'none';
//		}
	
} 

function changeClass(id){
	
	for(x = 2 ; x < 7 ; x++){
		if(x == id){
			document.getElementById('goto'+x).className = 'selected';
		} else {
			document.getElementById('goto'+x).className = 'Notselected';
		}
	}
	
}

function bigOne(obj){
	img = document.getElementById(obj).src;

	if(img.indexOf('On') != -1){imgFinal = img.replace('On','Of');}
	else{imgFinal = img.replace('Of','On');}

	document.getElementById(obj).src = imgFinal;
}

			<div class="book-info-about-audience float-right">
				<div class="book-info-bottom-indetail book-page-content float-right">
									<h2>Book Description</h2>
									<div class="book-info-bottom-indetail-text" itemprop="description">
										<p>Even with the rise of social media, forums remain a popular part of the Internet. bbPress allows you to increase interactivity with your WordPress website or blog by creating discussion forums within its confines.</p>
<p>bbPress Complete will show you how to create and manage a forum effectively. You will learn how to manage users, expand your forum with plugins, and integrate your forum into the rest of your site, whether it is a local community forum or a large website with thousands of visitors.</p>
<p>You will start off by learning the basics of bbPress and gradually acquire all the skills needed to run a successful bbPress community. You will learn how to integrate your forum effectively with the rest of your site, as well as how to manage the different kinds of users and much more. With clear, concise instructions detailing every aspect of the software, you will gain the knowledge required to extend bbPress using plugins and add bbPress to your WordPress theme. Furthermore, the real-world examples and clear instructions will give you all the tools you need to turn your blog into a successful community hub.</p>

									</div>

					<h2>What You Will Learn</h2>
					<div class="book-info-will-learn-text">
						<ul>
<li>Install bbPress on a WordPress installation and troubleshoot common problems</li>
<li>Manage posts, promote popular discussions, merge similar topics, and block spam, allowing your forum to grow</li>
<li>Expand the functionality of your forum with WordPress and bbPress plugins</li>
<li>Build specific templates using the WordPress and bbPress templating system</li>
<li>Give useful information by providing a sidebar in your forum</li>
</ul>

					<h2>Authors</h2>
					<div class="book-info-bottom-author-text">
						<div itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
						<div class="book-info-bottom-author-title" >
							<h3 itemprop="name">Rhys Wynne</h3>
						</div>

						<div class="book-info-bottom-author-body"  itemprop="description">
							Rhys Wynne is a web developer and Internet marketer originally from Colwyn Bay, North Wales, though now based in Manchester. Rhys has over seven years of commercial experience in developing websites, the majority of which have been built in WordPress. Rhys has over three years of experience in developing bbPress websites, and has released a number of plugins both for free and for commercial use. One such plugin, WP Email Capture, has been downloaded nearly 100,000 times.

Apart from Internet technologies, Rhys is a keen football fan, supporting his hometown team of Colwyn Bay, and he also enjoys traveling and photography.
